msg:One of the most satisfying hotels I have stayed in in recent years, it can be said to be a substitute for Yangzhou Guest House.
It took an hour and a half to drive from Shanghai. The navigation seemed to be a little inaccurate. Just drive in when you see the main entrance.
The garden-style design, one step at a time, the landscaping is very delicate. It takes about an hour to walk around slowly. There is also a small door leading directly to the Nanhu Scenic Area.
I asked for a quiet room. Although it was on the first floor, it was really quiet. I rested well at night. The room was cleaned without dead corners. The cleaning aunties all wore headgear, which was a good comment.
The breakfast variety is rich and the taste is good. The Western style feels better than the Chinese style. The coffee is rich, the milk and tea are very hot, and there are at least 8-9 kinds of fruits. Every day starts a day full of vitality. The details are also well done. I saw that the staff even changed the plates outside for food clips.
There are always staff in the lobby ready to solve your needs at any time.
The Chinese restaurant is also delicious. Although it may be a bit salty due to the cuisine, the flaws do not cover the merits. I ate in the hotel for two days.
If I really want to nitpick, the air conditioner in the room is a bit loud. It is still quite loud even at the lowest setting. It would be perfect if it could be adjusted.
I plan to stay here for a few days every year. I look forward to seeing you next time.

The rooms in Buildings 3 and 6 seem to be more advanced and the landscaping next to them is better. We may consider them next time.

posted:Posted October 22, 2023
msg:In order to visit the Nanhu Scenic Area, I stayed at the Nanhu Hotel for two nights over the weekend. I often stay in hotels, so this review is to compare with other hotels of the same level. As the State Guesthouse in Jiaxing, compared with the Xijiao Hotel in Shanghai, the West Lake State Guesthouse in Hangzhou, and the Jinji Lake Hotel in Suzhou, it is a new hotel with new and complete facilities and better catering. Among the four hotels, the buffet breakfast is the best. A good family. I can‚Äôt comment on the buffet dinner because I didn‚Äôt make a reservation in advance (you need to make a reservation a week in advance). After eating a la carte Japanese food, the dishes are still a bit different from those of the Black Pearl Japanese Food Store in Shanghai, although the prices are almost the same. Room condition: The sound insulation is good, there is a smart toilet, a capsule coffee machine, a spacious sink, and soft room lighting, but the air conditioner is relatively loud. Service: The staff are very good, and the aunt who cleans the room also says hello. Garden view: The hotel's own garden is small, incomparable to the other three state hotels mentioned above, and can basically be ignored, because it is adjacent to the Nanhu Scenic Area and is supplemented, so it is okay. When walking around the garden, there are dead ends, such as walking through a cave and arriving at Building 7. The door is locked and guests need to go back the same way. This doesn't feel good. I would like to make two suggestions. One is that the pillow selection list should be placed on the bedside table so that guests can see it at a glance, rather than putting it in a book on the square table. I think many guests may not find this list when they check out. Because the pillows are really soft, I always bring my own pillows in the car and put them in the room. When I was browsing after taking a shower at night, I discovered that there was a pillow menu and not placed on the bedside table. Is this to reduce the workload of the waiter? Second point, it is best for the hotel to add reminders about taking a boat trip to the Nanhu Lake Scenic Area. Guests come to stay at your house to visit the Nanhu Lake. There are three piers in Nanhu. Only Huijingyuan Pier can take you to and from Huxin Island for 20 yuan. The other two piers cost 60 yuan to go around the lake and then go to Huijingyuan Pier to transfer to the ferry boat to Huxin Island. And this The 60 yuan ferry ticket must be booked on the spot by scanning the QR code at the pier. It is not available on Ctrip. On weekend afternoons, the ticket is often fully booked and not available. The longest walk to Huijingyuan Pier takes 40 minutes. It takes 20 minutes to walk back to the hotel from Nanhu Tiandi Pier. It takes about 2 hours to walk around Nanhu (stop and go). You must queue up at Huijingyuan Pier to go to the lake center island. Otherwise, like me, I felt that there were too many people in line at Huijingyuan Pier and wanted to go to the next one. I took a boat at the pier, and then I was fooled. After walking around, I went back to the tower in front of the hotel and bought a 60 yuan boat ticket. I took the wrong path and spent the wrong money just to get an island in the middle of the lake.
